# Comments for Question 2, LLM=Grok 2 12-12

== Grader: Claude 3.7 Sonnet ==
  * grade_story_100.txt (grade=5.8)
    The plot has a clear arc with beginning, middle, and resolution, but relies too heavily on telling rather than showing key developments. The cosmic deception remains abstract rather than concrete, weakening the stakes. While the pressed pennies create a tangible quest structure, the revelation at the climax feels rushed and underexplained. The connection between the impending apology and the cosmic deception lacks sufficient development to feel cohesive.

  * grade_story_103.txt (grade=3.8)
    The plot lacks coherence and clear causality. The story builds toward a climactic decision that's ultimately withheld from the reader, creating an unsatisfying non-resolution. The random items pattern mechanism feels underdeveloped and arbitrary rather than integral to the plot.

The resolution comes too easily, with Alex simply pulling the last knot without meaningful struggle or complication.
